NOTIFICATIONS BY THE ELECTION COMMISSION OF INDIA
AMENDMENT TO THE LIST OF ASSISTANT ELECTORAL REGISTRATION OFFICERS FOR 
THE ASSEMBLY CONSTITUENCIES IN THE STATE OF TAMIL NADU.
No. SRO G-37/2025.
The following Notification of the Election Commission of India, Nirvachan Sadan, Ashoka Road, New Delhi-110 001, 
dated 28th November, 2025 [07 Agrahayan, Saka (1947)] is published:-
No.  429/TN/2025 (2).-  In exercise  of the powers conferred by  sub-section (1) of Section 13 (C) of the Representation 
of the People Act, 1950 (43 of 1950), the Election Commission of India hereby makes the following amendment in the 
Notification No. 429/TN/2025(2) dated 08.05.2025 as amended from time to time, relating to designating Assistant Electoral 
Registration Officers for Assembly Constituencies in the State of  Tamil Nadu, namely:-

Constituency shown in the column (1), the following entry shall be added:
